     1	/** @import { Pattern } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../types' */
     4	import { dev } from '../../../../state.js';
     5	import { extract_identifiers } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
     6	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
     7	import { create_derived } from '../utils.js';
     8	import { get_value } from './shared/declarations.js';
     9	import { build_expression } from './shared/utils.js';
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * @param {AST.ConstTag} node
    13	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    14	 */
    15	export function ConstTag(node, context) {
    16	        const declaration = node.declaration.declarations[0];
    17	        // TODO we can almost certainly share some code with $derived(...)
    18	        if (declaration.id.type === 'Identifier') {
    19	                const init = build_expression(context, declaration.init, node.metadata.expression);
    20	                let expression = create_derived(context.state, b.thunk(init));
    21	
    22	                if (dev) {
    23	                        expression = b.call('$.tag', expression, b.literal(declaration.id.name));
    24	                }
    25	
    26	                context.state.init.push(b.const(declaration.id, expression));
    27	
    28	                context.state.transform[declaration.id.name] = { read: get_value };
    29	
    30	                // we need to eagerly evaluate the expression in order to hit any
    31	                // 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
    32	                if (dev) {
    33	                        context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.get', declaration.id)));
    34	                }
    35	        } else {
    36	                const identifiers = extract_identifiers(declaration.id);
    37	                const tmp = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('computed_const'));
    38	
    39	                const transform = { ...context.state.transform };
    40	
    41	                // Make all identifiers that are declared within the following computed regular
    42	                // variables, as they are not signals in that context yet
    43	                for (const node of identifiers) {
    44	                        delete transform[node.name];
    45	                }
    46	
    47	                const child_state = { ...context.state, transform };
    48	
    49	                // TODO optimise the simple `{ x } = y` case — we can just return `y`
    50	                // instead of destructuring it only to return a new object
    51	                const init = build_expression(
    52	                        { ...context, state: child_state },
    53	                        declaration.init,
    54	                        node.metadata.expression
    55	                );
    56	                const fn = b.arrow(
    57	                        [],
    58	                        b.block([
    59	                                b.const(/** @type {Pattern} */ (context.visit(declaration.id, child_state)), init),
    60	                                b.return(b.object(identifiers.map((node) => b.prop('init', node, node))))
    61	                        ])
    62	                );
    63	
    64	                let expression = create_derived(context.state, fn);
    65	
    66	                if (dev) {
    67	                        expression = b.call('$.tag', expression, b.literal('[@const]'));
    68	                }
    69	
    70	                context.state.init.push(b.const(tmp, expression));
    71	
    72	                // we need to eagerly evaluate the expression in order to hit any
    73	                // 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
    74	                if (dev) {
    75	                        context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.get', tmp)));
    76	                }
    77	
    78	                for (const node of identifiers) {
    79	                        context.state.transform[node.name] = {
    80	                                read: (node) => b.member(b.call('$.get', tmp), node)
    81	                        };
    82	                }
    83	        }
    84	}

     1	/** @import { ArrowFunctionExpression, AssignmentExpression, Expression, FunctionDeclaration, FunctionExpression, Identifier, Node, Pattern, UpdateExpression } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { Binding } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ClientTransformState, ComponentClientTransformState, ComponentContext } from './types.js' */
     4	/** @import { Analysis } from '../../types.js' */
     5	/** @import { Scope } from '../../scope.js' */
     6	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
     7	import { is_simple_expression } from '../../../utils/ast.js';
     8	import {
     9	        PROPS_IS_LAZY_INITIAL,
    10	        PROPS_IS_IMMUTABLE,
    11	        PROPS_IS_RUNES,
    12	        PROPS_IS_UPDATED,
    13	        PROPS_IS_BINDABLE
    14	} from '../../../../constants.js';
    15	import { dev } from '../../../state.js';
    16	import { walk } from 'zimmerframe';
    17	import { validate_mutation } from './visitors/shared/utils.js';
    18	
    19	/**
    20	 * @param {Binding} binding
    21	 * @param {Analysis} analysis
    22	 * @returns {boolean}
    23	 */
    24	export function is_state_source(binding, analysis) {
    25	        return (
    26	                (binding.kind === 'state' || binding.kind === 'raw_state') &&
    27	                (!analysis.immutable || binding.reassigned || analysis.accessors)
    28	        );
    29	}
    30	
    31	/**
    32	 * @param {Identifier} node
    33	 * @param {ClientTransformState} state
    34	 * @returns {Expression}
    35	 */
    36	export function build_getter(node, state) {
    37	        if (Object.hasOwn(state.transform, node.name)) {
    38	                const binding = state.scope.get(node.name);
    39	
    40	                // don't transform the declaration itself
    41	                if (node !== binding?.node) {
    42	                        return state.transform[node.name].read(node);
    43	                }
    44	        }
    45	
    46	        return node;
    47	}
    48	
    49	/**
    50	 * @param {FunctionDeclaration | FunctionExpression | ArrowFunctionExpression} node
    51	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    52	 * @returns {Pattern[]}
    53	 */
    54	function get_hoisted_params(node, context) {
    55	        const scope = context.state.scope;
    56	
    57	        /** @type {Identifier[]} */
    58	        const params = [];
    59	
    60	        /**
    61	         * We only want to push if it's not already present to avoid name clashing
    62	         * @param {Identifier} id
    63	         */
    64	        function push_unique(id) {
    65	                if (!params.find((param) => param.name === id.name)) {
    66	                        params.push(id);
    67	                }
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
    71	                let binding = scope.get(reference);
    72	
    73	                if (binding !== null && !scope.declarations.has(reference) && binding.initial !== node) {
    74	                        if (binding.kind === 'store_sub') {
    75	                                // We need both the subscription for getting the value and the store for updating
    76	                                push_unique(b.id(binding.node.name));
    77	                                binding = /** @type {Binding} */ (scope.get(binding.node.name.slice(1)));
    78	                        }
    79	
    80	                        let expression = context.state.transform[reference]?.read(b.id(binding.node.name));
    81	
    82	                        if (
    83	                                // If it's a destructured derived binding, then we can extract the derived signal reference and use that.
    84	                                // TODO this code is bad, we need to kill it
    85	                                expression != null &&
    86	                                typeof expression !== 'function' &&
    87	                                expression.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    88	                                expression.object.type === 'CallExpression' &&
    89	                                expression.object.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    90	                                expression.object.callee.name === '$.get' &&
    91	                                expression.object.arguments[0].type === 'Identifier'
    92	                        ) {
    93	                                push_unique(b.id(expression.object.arguments[0].name));
    94	                        } else if (
    95	                                // If we are referencing a simple $$props value, then we need to reference the object property instead
    96	                                (binding.kind === 'prop' || binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') &&
    97	                                !is_prop_source(binding, context.state)
    98	                        ) {
    99	                                push_unique(b.id('$$props'));
   100	                        } else if (
   101	                                // imports don't need to be hoisted
   102	                                binding.declaration_kind !== 'import'
   103	                        ) {
   104	                                // create a copy to remove start/end tags which would mess up source maps
   105	                                push_unique(b.id(binding.node.name));
   106	                                // rest props are often accessed through the $$props object for optimization reasons,
   107	                                // but we can't know if the delegated event handler will use it, so we need to add both as params
   108	                                if (binding.kind === 'rest_prop' && context.state.analysis.runes) {
   109	                                        push_unique(b.id('$$props'));
   110	                                }
   111	                        }
   112	                }
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        if (dev) {
   116	                // this is a little hacky, but necessary for ownership validation
   117	                // to work inside hoisted event handlers
   118	
   119	                /**
   120	                 * @param {AssignmentExpression | UpdateExpression} node
   121	                 * @param {{ next: () => void, stop: () => void }} context
   122	                 */
   123	                function visit(node, { next, stop }) {
   124	                        if (validate_mutation(node, /** @type {any} */ (context), node) !== node) {
   125	                                params.push(b.id('$$ownership_validator'));
   126	                                stop();
   127	                        } else {
   128	                                next();
   129	                        }
   130	                }
   131	
   132	                walk(/** @type {Node} */ (node), null, {
   133	                        AssignmentExpression: visit,
   134	                        UpdateExpression: visit
   135	                });
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        return params;
   139	}
   140	
   141	/**
   142	 * @param {FunctionDeclaration | FunctionExpression | ArrowFunctionExpression} node
   143	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   144	 * @returns {Pattern[]}
   145	 */
   146	export function build_hoisted_params(node, context) {
   147	        const hoisted_params = get_hoisted_params(node, context);
   148	        node.metadata.hoisted_params = hoisted_params;
   149	
   150	        /** @type {Pattern[]} */
   151	        const params = [];
   152	
   153	        if (node.params.length === 0) {
   154	                if (hoisted_params.length > 0) {
   155	                        // For the event object
   156	                        params.push(b.id(context.state.scope.generate('_')));
   157	                }
   158	        } else {
   159	                for (const param of node.params) {
   160	                        params.push(/** @type {Pattern} */ (context.visit(param)));
   161	                }
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        params.push(...hoisted_params);
   165	        return params;
   166	}
   167	
   168	/**
   169	 * @param {Binding} binding
   170	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
   171	 * @param {string} name
   172	 * @param {Expression | null} [initial]
   173	 * @returns
   174	 */
   175	export function get_prop_source(binding, state, name, initial) {
   176	        /** @type {Expression[]} */
   177	        const args = [b.id('$$props'), b.literal(name)];
   178	
   179	        let flags = 0;
   180	
   181	        if (binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') {
   182	                flags |= PROPS_IS_BINDABLE;
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        if (state.analysis.immutable) {
   186	                flags |= PROPS_IS_IMMUTABLE;
   187	        }
   188	
   189	        if (state.analysis.runes) {
   190	                flags |= PROPS_IS_RUNES;
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        if (
   194	                state.analysis.accessors ||
   195	                (state.analysis.immutable
   196	                        ? binding.reassigned || (state.analysis.runes && binding.mutated)
   197	                        : binding.updated)
   198	        ) {
   199	                flags |= PROPS_IS_UPDATED;
   200	        }
   201	
   202	        /** @type {Expression | undefined} */
   203	        let arg;
   204	
   205	        if (initial) {
   206	                // To avoid eagerly evaluating the right-hand-side, we wrap it in a thunk if necessary
   207	                if (is_simple_expression(initial)) {
   208	                        arg = initial;
   209	                } else {
   210	                        if (
   211	                                initial.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   212	                                initial.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
   213	                                initial.arguments.length === 0
   214	                        ) {
   215	                                arg = initial.callee;
   216	                        } else {
   217	                                arg = b.thunk(initial);
   218	                        }
   219	
   220	                        flags |= PROPS_IS_LAZY_INITIAL;
   221	                }
   222	        }
   223	
   224	        if (flags || arg) {
   225	                args.push(b.literal(flags));
   226	                if (arg) args.push(arg);
   227	        }
   228	
   229	        return b.call('$.prop', ...args);
   230	}
   231	
   232	/**
   233	 *
   234	 * @param {Binding} binding
   235	 * @param {ClientTransformState} state
   236	 * @returns
   237	 */
   238	export function is_prop_source(binding, state) {
   239	        return (
   240	                (binding.kind === 'prop' || binding.kind === 'bindable_prop') &&
   241	                (!state.analysis.runes ||
   242	                        state.analysis.accessors ||
   243	                        binding.reassigned ||
   244	                        binding.initial ||
   245	                        // Until legacy mode is gone, we also need to use the prop source when only mutated is true,
   246	                        // because the parent could be a legacy component which needs coarse-grained reactivity
   247	                        binding.updated)
   248	        );
   249	}
   250	
   251	/**
   252	 * @param {Expression} node
   253	 * @param {Scope | null} scope
   254	 */
   255	export function should_proxy(node, scope) {
   256	        if (
   257	                !node ||
   258	                node.type === 'Literal' ||
   259	                node.type === 'TemplateLiteral' ||
   260	                node.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' ||
   261	                node.type === 'FunctionExpression' ||
   262	                node.type === 'UnaryExpression' ||
   263	                node.type === 'BinaryExpression' ||
   264	                (node.type === 'Identifier' && node.name === 'undefined')
   265	        ) {
   266	                return false;
   267	        }
   268	
   269	        if (node.type === 'Identifier' && scope !== null) {
   270	                const binding = scope.get(node.name);
   271	                // Let's see if the reference is something that can be proxied
   272	                if (
   273	                        binding !== null &&
   274	                        !binding.reassigned &&
   275	                        binding.initial !== null &&
   276	                        binding.initial.type !== 'FunctionDeclaration' &&
   277	                        binding.initial.type !== 'ClassDeclaration' &&
   278	                        binding.initial.type !== 'ImportDeclaration' &&
   279	                        binding.initial.type !== 'EachBlock' &&
   280	                        binding.initial.type !== 'SnippetBlock'
   281	                ) {
   282	                        return should_proxy(binding.initial, null);
   283	                }
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        return true;
   287	}
   288	
   289	/**
   290	 * Svelte legacy mode should use safe equals in most places, runes mode shouldn't
   291	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
   292	 * @param {Expression} arg
   293	 */
   294	export function create_derived(state, arg) {
   295	        return b.call(state.analysis.runes ? '$.derived' : '$.derived_safe_equal', arg);
   296	}

    59	                        throw new TypeError('Template must be a string');
    60	                }
    61

    63	                this.template = template.trimEnd();

    66

    98	                }

   170	        eat(str, required = false, required_in_loose = true) {
   171	                if (this.match(str)) {
   172	                        this.index += str.length;
   173	                        return true;
   174	                }
   175	
   176	                if (required && (!this.loose || required_in_loose)) {
   177	                        e.expected_token(this.index, str);
   178	                }

   183	        /** @param {string} str */
   184	        match(str) {
   185	                const length = str.length;
   186	                if (length === 1) {
   187	                        // more performant than slicing
   188	                        return this.template[this.index] === str;
   189	                }
   190	
   191	                return this.template.slice(this.index, this.index + length) === str;
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        /**
   195	         * Match a regex at the current index
   196	         * @param {RegExp} pattern  Should have a ^ anchor at the start so the regex doesn't search past the beginning, resulting in worse performance
   197	         */
   198	        match_regex(pattern) {
   199	                const match = pattern.exec(this.template.slice(this.index));
   200	                if (!match || match.index !== 0) return null;
   201	
   202	                return match[0];
   203	        }
   204	
   205	        allow_whitespace() {
   206	                while (this.index < this.template.length && regex_whitespace.test(this.template[this.index])) {
   207	                        this.index++;
   208	                }
   209	        }
   210	
   211	        /**
   212	         * Search for a regex starting at the current index and return the result if it matches
   213	         * @param {RegExp} pattern  Should have a ^ anchor at the start so the regex doesn't search past the beginning, resulting in worse performance
   214	         */
   215	        read(pattern) {
   216	                const result = this.match_regex(pattern);
   217	                if (result) this.index += result.length;
   218	                return result;
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        /** @param {any} allow_reserved */
   222	        read_identifier(allow_reserved = false) {
   223	                const start = this.index;
   224	
   225	                let i = this.index;
   226	
   227	                const code = /** @type {number} */ (this.template.codePointAt(i));
   228	                if (!isIdentifierStart(code, true)) return null;
   229	
   230	                i += code <= 0xffff ? 1 : 2;
   231	
   232	                while (i < this.template.length) {
   233	                        const code = /** @type {number} */ (this.template.codePointAt(i));
   234	
   235	                        if (!isIdentifierChar(code, true)) break;
   236	                        i += code <= 0xffff ? 1 : 2;
   237	                }
   238	
   239	                const identifier = this.template.slice(this.index, (this.index = i));
   240	
   241	                if (!allow_reserved && is_reserved(identifier)) {
   242	                        e.unexpected_reserved_word(start, identifier);
   243	                }
   244	
   245	                return identifier;
   246	        }
   247	
   248	        /** @param {RegExp} pattern */
   249	        read_until(pattern) {
   250	                if (this.index >= this.template.length) {
   251	                        if (this.loose) return '';
   252	                        e.unexpected_eof(this.template.length);
   253	                }
   254	
   255	                const start = this.index;
   256	                const match = pattern.exec(this.template.slice(start));
   257	
   258	                if (match) {
   259	                        this.index = start + match.index;
   260	                        return this.template.slice(start, this.index);
   261	                }
   262	
   263	                this.index = this.template.length;
   264	                return this.template.slice(start);
   265	        }
   266	
   267	        require_whitespace() {
   268	                if (!regex_whitespace.test(this.template[this.index])) {
   269	                        e.expected_whitespace(this.index);
   270	                }
   271	
   272	                this.allow_whitespace();
   273	        }
   274	
   275	        pop() {
   276	                this.fragments.pop();
   277	                return this.stack.pop();
   278	        }
   279	
   280	        /**
   281	         * @template {AST.Fragment['nodes'][number]} T
   282	         * @param {T} node
   283	         * @returns {T}
   284	         */
   285	        append(node) {
   286	                this.fragments.at(-1)?.nodes.push(node);
   287	                return node;
   288	        }
   289	}

   291	/**
   292	 * @param {string} template
   293	 * @param {boolean} [loose]
   294	 * @returns {AST.Root}
   295	 */
   296	export function parse(template, loose = false) {
   297	        state.set_source(template);
   298	
   299	        const parser = new Parser(template, loose);
   300	        return parser.root;
   301	}

     1	/** @import { Expression } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { Parser } from '../index.js' */
     3	import { parse_expression_at } from '../acorn.js';
     4	import { regex_whitespace } from '../../patterns.js';
     5	import * as e from '../../../errors.js';
     6	import { find_matching_bracket } from '../utils/bracket.js';
     7	
     8	/**
     9	 * @param {Parser} parser
    10	 * @param {string} [opening_token]
    11	 * @returns {Expression | undefined}
    12	 */
    13	export function get_loose_identifier(parser, opening_token) {
    14	        // Find the next } and treat it as the end of the expression
    15	        const end = find_matching_bracket(parser.template, parser.index, opening_token ?? '{');
    16	        if (end) {
    17	                const start = parser.index;
    18	                parser.index = end;
    19	                // We don't know what the expression is and signal this by returning an empty identifier
    20	                return {
    21	                        type: 'Identifier',
    22	                        start,
    23	                        end,
    24	                        name: ''
    25	                };
    26	        }
    27	}
    28	
    29	/**
    30	 * @param {Parser} parser
    31	 * @param {string} [opening_token]
    32	 * @param {boolean} [disallow_loose]
    33	 * @returns {Expression}
    34	 */
    35	export default function read_expression(parser, opening_token, disallow_loose) {
    36	        try {
    37	                let comment_index = parser.root.comments.length;
    38	
    39	                const node = parse_expression_at(
    40	                        parser.template,
    41	                        parser.root.comments,
    42	                        parser.ts,
    43	                        parser.index
    44	                );
    45	
    46	                let num_parens = 0;
    47	
    48	                let i = parser.root.comments.length;
    49	                while (i-- > comment_index) {
    50	                        const comment = parser.root.comments[i];
    51	                        if (comment.end < node.start) {
    52	                                parser.index = comment.end;
    53	                                break;
    54	                        }
    55	                }
    56	
    57	                for (let i = parser.index; i < /** @type {number} */ (node.start); i += 1) {
    58	                        if (parser.template[i] === '(') num_parens += 1;
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                let index = /** @type {number} */ (node.end);
    62	
    63	                const last_comment = parser.root.comments.at(-1);
    64	                if (last_comment && last_comment.end > index) index = last_comment.end;
    65	
    66	                while (num_parens > 0) {
    67	                        const char = parser.template[index];
    68	
    69	                        if (char === ')') {
    70	                                num_parens -= 1;
    71	                        } else if (!regex_whitespace.test(char)) {
    72	                                e.expected_token(index, ')');
    73	                        }
    74	
    75	                        index += 1;
    76	                }
    77	
    78	                parser.index = index;
    79	
    80	                return /** @type {Expression} */ (node);
    81	        } catch (err) {
    82	                // If we are in an each loop we need the error to be thrown in cases like
    83	                // `as { y = z }` so we still throw and handle the error there
    84	                if (parser.loose && !disallow_loose) {
    85	                        const expression = get_loose_identifier(parser, opening_token);
    86	                        if (expression) {
    87	                                return expression;
    88	                        }
    89	                }
    90	
    91	                parser.acorn_error(err);
    92	        }
    93	}
    94

    18	export default function tag(parser) {
    19	        const start = parser.index;
    20	        parser.index += 1;
    21	
    22	        parser.allow_whitespace();

    25	        if (parser.eat(':')) return next(parser);
    26	        if (parser.eat('@')) return special(parser);

    31	                }

    40	                type: 'ExpressionTag',

    50	/** @param {Parser} parser */
    51	function open(parser) {
    52	        let start = parser.index - 2;
    53	        while (parser.template[start] !== '{') start -= 1;
    54	
    55	        if (parser.eat('if')) {
    56	                parser.require_whitespace();
    57	
    58	                /** @type {AST.IfBlock} */
    59	                const block = parser.append({
    60	                        type: 'IfBlock',
    61	                        elseif: false,
    62	                        start,
    63	                        end: -1,
    64	                        test: read_expression(parser),
    65	                        consequent: create_fragment(),
    66	                        alternate: null,
    67	                        metadata: {
    68	                                expression: create_expression_metadata()
    69	                        }
    70	                });
    71	
    72	                parser.allow_whitespace();
    73	                parser.eat('}', true);
    74	
    75	                parser.stack.push(block);
    76	                parser.fragments.push(block.consequent);
    77	
    78	                return;
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        if (parser.eat('each')) {
    82	                parser.require_whitespace();
    83	
    84	                const template = parser.template;
    85	                let end = parser.template.length;
    86	
    87	                /** @type {Expression | undefined} */
    88	                let expression;
    89	
    90	                // we have to do this loop because `{#each x as { y = z }}` fails to parse —
    91	                // the `as { y = z }` is treated as an Expression but it's actually a Pattern.
    92	                // the 'fix' is to backtrack and hide everything from the `as` onwards, until
    93	                // we get a valid expression
    94	                while (!expression) {
    95	                        try {
    96	                                expression = read_expression(parser, undefined, true);
    97	                        } catch (err) {
    98	                                end = /** @type {any} */ (err).position[0] - 2;
    99	
   100	                                while (end > start && parser.template.slice(end, end + 2) !== 'as') {
   101	                                        end -= 1;
   102	                                }
   103	
   104	                                if (end <= start) {
   105	                                        if (parser.loose) {
   106	                                                expression = get_loose_identifier(parser);
   107	                                                if (expression) {
   108	                                                        break;
   109	                                                }
   110	                                        }
   111	                                        throw err;
   112	                                }
   113	
   114	                                // @ts-expect-error parser.template is meant to be readonly, this is a special case
   115	                                parser.template = template.slice(0, end);
   116	                        }
   117	                }
   118	
   119	                // @ts-expect-error
   120	                parser.template = template;
   121	
   122	                parser.allow_whitespace();
   123	
   124	                // {#each} blocks must declare a context – {#each list as item}
   125	                if (!parser.match('as')) {
   126	                        // this could be a TypeScript assertion that was erroneously eaten.
   127	
   128	                        if (expression.type === 'SequenceExpression') {
   129	                                expression = expression.expressions[0];
   130	                        }
   131	
   132	                        let assertion = null;
   133	                        let end = expression.end;
   134	
   135	                        expression = walk(expression, null, {
   136	                                // @ts-expect-error
   137	                                TSAsExpression(node, context) {
   138	                                        if (node.end === /** @type {Expression} */ (expression).end) {
   139	                                                assertion = node;
   140	                                                end = node.expression.end;
   141	                                                return node.expression;
   142	                                        }
   143	
   144	                                        context.next();
   145	                                }
   146	                        });
   147	
   148	                        expression.end = end;
   149	
   150	                        if (assertion) {
   151	                                // we can't reset `parser.index` to `expression.expression.end` because
   152	                                // it will ignore any parentheses — we need to jump through this hoop
   153	                                let end = /** @type {any} */ (/** @type {any} */ (assertion).typeAnnotation).start - 2;
   154	                                while (parser.template.slice(end, end + 2) !== 'as') end -= 1;
   155	
   156	                                parser.index = end;
   157	                        }
   158	                }
   159	
   160	                /** @type {Pattern | null} */
   161	                let context = null;
   162	                let index;
   163	                let key;
   164	
   165	                if (parser.eat('as')) {
   166	                        parser.require_whitespace();
   167	
   168	                        context = read_pattern(parser);
   169	                } else {
   170	                        // {#each Array.from({ length: 10 }), i} is read as a sequence expression,
   171	                        // which is set back above - we now gotta reset the index as a consequence
   172	                        // to properly read the , i part
   173	                        parser.index = /** @type {number} */ (expression.end);
   174	                }
   175	
   176	                parser.allow_whitespace();
   177	
   178	                if (parser.eat(',')) {
   179	                        parser.allow_whitespace();
   180	                        index = parser.read_identifier();
   181	                        if (!index) {
   182	                                e.expected_identifier(parser.index);
   183	                        }
   184	
   185	                        parser.allow_whitespace();
   186	                }
   187	
   188	                if (parser.eat('(')) {
   189	                        parser.allow_whitespace();
   190	
   191	                        key = read_expression(parser, '(');
   192	                        parser.allow_whitespace();
   193	                        parser.eat(')', true);
   194	                        parser.allow_whitespace();
   195	                }
   196	
   197	                const matches = parser.eat('}', true, false);
   198	
   199	                if (!matches) {
   200	                        // Parser may have read the `as` as part of the expression (e.g. in `{#each foo. as x}`)
   201	                        if (parser.template.slice(parser.index - 4, parser.index) === ' as ') {
   202	                                const prev_index = parser.index;
   203	                                context = read_pattern(parser);
   204	                                parser.eat('}', true);
   205	                                expression = {
   206	                                        type: 'Identifier',
   207	                                        name: '',
   208	                                        start: expression.start,
   209	                                        end: prev_index - 4
   210	                                };
   211	                        } else {
   212	                                parser.eat('}', true); // rerun to produce the parser error
   213	                        }
   214	                }
   215	
   216	                /** @type {AST.EachBlock} */
   217	                const block = parser.append({
   218	                        type: 'EachBlock',
   219	                        start,
   220	                        end: -1,
   221	                        expression,
   222	                        body: create_fragment(),
   223	                        context,
   224	                        index,
   225	                        key,
   226	                        metadata: /** @type {any} */ (null) // filled in later
   227	                });
   228	
   229	                parser.stack.push(block);
   230	                parser.fragments.push(block.body);
   231	
   232	                return;
   233	        }
   234	
   235	        if (parser.eat('await')) {
   236	                parser.require_whitespace();
   237	                const expression = read_expression(parser);
   238	                parser.allow_whitespace();
   239	
   240	                /** @type {AST.AwaitBlock} */
   241	                const block = parser.append({
   242	                        type: 'AwaitBlock',
   243	                        start,
   244	                        end: -1,
   245	                        expression,
   246	                        value: null,
   247	                        error: null,
   248	                        pending: null,
   249	                        then: null,
   250	                        catch: null,
   251	                        metadata: {
   252	                                expression: create_expression_metadata()
   253	                        }
   254	                });
   255	
   256	                if (parser.eat('then')) {
   257	                        if (parser.match_regex(regex_whitespace_with_closing_curly_brace)) {
   258	                                parser.allow_whitespace();
   259	                        } else {
   260	                                parser.require_whitespace();
   261	                                block.value = read_pattern(parser);
   262	                                parser.allow_whitespace();
   263	                        }
   264	
   265	                        block.then = create_fragment();
   266	                        parser.fragments.push(block.then);
   267	                } else if (parser.eat('catch')) {
   268	                        if (parser.match_regex(regex_whitespace_with_closing_curly_brace)) {
   269	                                parser.allow_whitespace();
   270	                        } else {
   271	                                parser.require_whitespace();
   272	                                block.error = read_pattern(parser);
   273	                                parser.allow_whitespace();
   274	                        }
   275	
   276	                        block.catch = create_fragment();
   277	                        parser.fragments.push(block.catch);
   278	                } else {
   279	                        block.pending = create_fragment();
   280	                        parser.fragments.push(block.pending);
   281	                }
   282	
   283	                const matches = parser.eat('}', true, false);
   284	
   285	                // Parser may have read the `then/catch` as part of the expression (e.g. in `{#await foo. then x}`)
   286	                if (!matches) {
   287	                        if (parser.template.slice(parser.index - 6, parser.index) === ' then ') {
   288	                                const prev_index = parser.index;
   289	                                block.value = read_pattern(parser);
   290	                                parser.eat('}', true);
   291	                                block.expression = {
   292	                                        type: 'Identifier',
   293	                                        name: '',
   294	                                        start: expression.start,
   295	                                        end: prev_index - 6
   296	                                };
   297	                                block.then = block.pending;
   298	                                block.pending = null;
   299	                        } else if (parser.template.slice(parser.index - 7, parser.index) === ' catch ') {
   300	                                const prev_index = parser.index;
   301	                                block.error = read_pattern(parser);
   302	                                parser.eat('}', true);
   303	                                block.expression = {
   304	                                        type: 'Identifier',
   305	                                        name: '',
   306	                                        start: expression.start,
   307	                                        end: prev_index - 7
   308	                                };
   309	                                block.catch = block.pending;
   310	                                block.pending = null;
   311	                        } else {
   312	                                parser.eat('}', true); // rerun to produce the parser error
   313	                        }
   314	                }
   315	
   316	                parser.stack.push(block);
   317	
   318	                return;
   319	        }
   320	
   321	        if (parser.eat('key')) {
   322	                parser.require_whitespace();
   323	
   324	                const expression = read_expression(parser);
   325	                parser.allow_whitespace();
   326	
   327	                parser.eat('}', true);
   328	
   329	                /** @type {AST.KeyBlock} */
   330	                const block = parser.append({
   331	                        type: 'KeyBlock',
   332	                        start,
   333	                        end: -1,
   334	                        expression,
   335	                        fragment: create_fragment(),
   336	                        metadata: {
   337	                                expression: create_expression_metadata()
   338	                        }
   339	                });
   340	
   341	                parser.stack.push(block);
   342	                parser.fragments.push(block.fragment);
   343	
   344	                return;
   345	        }
   346	
   347	        if (parser.eat('snippet')) {
   348	                parser.require_whitespace();
   349	
   350	                const name_start = parser.index;
   351	                let name = parser.read_identifier();
   352	                const name_end = parser.index;
   353	
   354	                if (name === null) {
   355	                        if (parser.loose) {
   356	                                name = '';
   357	                        } else {
   358	                                e.expected_identifier(parser.index);
   359	                        }
   360	                }
   361	
   362	                parser.allow_whitespace();
   363	
   364	                const params_start = parser.index;
   365	
   366	                // snippets could have a generic signature, e.g. `#snippet foo<T>(...)`
   367	                /** @type {string | undefined} */
   368	                let type_params;
   369	
   370	                // if we match a generic opening
   371	                if (parser.ts && parser.match('<')) {
   372	                        const start = parser.index;
   373	                        const end = match_bracket(parser, start, pointy_bois);
   374	
   375	                        type_params = parser.template.slice(start + 1, end - 1);
   376	
   377	                        parser.index = end;
   378	                }
   379	
   380	                parser.allow_whitespace();
   381	
   382	                const matched = parser.eat('(', true, false);
   383	
   384	                if (matched) {
   385	                        let parentheses = 1;
   386	
   387	                        while (parser.index < parser.template.length && (!parser.match(')') || parentheses !== 1)) {
   388	                                if (parser.match('(')) parentheses++;
   389	                                if (parser.match(')')) parentheses--;
   390	                                parser.index += 1;
   391	                        }
   392	
   393	                        parser.eat(')', true);
   394	                }
   395	
   396	                const prelude = parser.template.slice(0, params_start).replace(/\S/g, ' ');
   397	                const params = parser.template.slice(params_start, parser.index);
   398	
   399	                let function_expression = matched
   400	                        ? /** @type {ArrowFunctionExpression} */ (
   401	                                        parse_expression_at(
   402	                                                prelude + `${params} => {}`,
   403	                                                parser.root.comments,
   404	                                                parser.ts,
   405	                                                params_start
   406	                                        )
   407	                                )
   408	                        : { params: [] };
   409	
   410	                parser.allow_whitespace();
   411	                parser.eat('}', true);
   412	
   413	                /** @type {AST.SnippetBlock} */
   414	                const block = parser.append({
   415	                        type: 'SnippetBlock',
   416	                        start,
   417	                        end: -1,
   418	                        expression: {
   419	                                type: 'Identifier',
   420	                                start: name_start,
   421	                                end: name_end,
   422	                                name
   423	                        },
   424	                        typeParams: type_params,
   425	                        parameters: function_expression.params,
   426	                        body: create_fragment(),
   427	                        metadata: {
   428	                                can_hoist: false,
   429	                                sites: new Set()
   430	                        }
   431	                });
   432	                parser.stack.push(block);
   433	                parser.fragments.push(block.body);
   434	
   435	                return;
   436	        }
   437	
   438	        e.expected_block_type(parser.index);
   439	}
   440	
   441	/** @param {Parser} parser */
   442	function next(parser) {
   443	        const start = parser.index - 1;
   444	
   445	        const block = parser.current(); // TODO type should not be TemplateNode, that's much too broad
   446	
   447	        if (block.type === 'IfBlock') {
   448	                if (!parser.eat('else')) e.expected_token(start, '{:else} or {:else if}');
   449	                if (parser.eat('if')) e.block_invalid_elseif(start);
   450	
   451	                parser.allow_whitespace();
   452	
   453	                parser.fragments.pop();
   454	
   455	                block.alternate = create_fragment();
   456	                parser.fragments.push(block.alternate);
   457	
   458	                // :else if
   459	                if (parser.eat('if')) {
   460	                        parser.require_whitespace();
   461	
   462	                        const expression = read_expression(parser);
   463	
   464	                        parser.allow_whitespace();
   465	                        parser.eat('}', true);
   466	
   467	                        let elseif_start = start - 1;
   468	                        while (parser.template[elseif_start] !== '{') elseif_start -= 1;
   469	
   470	                        /** @type {AST.IfBlock} */
   471	                        const child = parser.append({
   472	                                start: elseif_start,
   473	                                end: -1,
   474	                                type: 'IfBlock',
   475	                                elseif: true,
   476	                                test: expression,
   477	                                consequent: create_fragment(),
   478	                                alternate: null,
   479	                                metadata: {
   480	                                        expression: create_expression_metadata()
   481	                                }
   482	                        });
   483	
   484	                        parser.stack.push(child);
   485	                        parser.fragments.pop();
   486	                        parser.fragments.push(child.consequent);
   487	                } else {
   488	                        // :else
   489	                        parser.allow_whitespace();
   490	                        parser.eat('}', true);
   491	                }
   492	
   493	                return;
   494	        }
   495	
   496	        if (block.type === 'EachBlock') {
   497	                if (!parser.eat('else')) e.expected_token(start, '{:else}');
   498	
   499	                parser.allow_whitespace();
   500	                parser.eat('}', true);
   501	
   502	                block.fallback = create_fragment();
   503	
   504	                parser.fragments.pop();
   505	                parser.fragments.push(block.fallback);
   506	
   507	                return;
   508	        }
   509	
   510	        if (block.type === 'AwaitBlock') {
   511	                if (parser.eat('then')) {
   512	                        if (block.then) {
   513	                                e.block_duplicate_clause(start, '{:then}');
   514	                        }
   515	
   516	                        if (!parser.eat('}')) {
   517	                                parser.require_whitespace();
   518	                                block.value = read_pattern(parser);
   519	                                parser.allow_whitespace();
   520	                                parser.eat('}', true);
   521	                        }
   522	
   523	                        block.then = create_fragment();
   524	                        parser.fragments.pop();
   525	                        parser.fragments.push(block.then);
   526	
   527	                        return;
   528	                }
   529	
   530	                if (parser.eat('catch')) {
   531	                        if (block.catch) {
   532	                                e.block_duplicate_clause(start, '{:catch}');
   533	                        }
   534	
   535	                        if (!parser.eat('}')) {
   536	                                parser.require_whitespace();
   537	                                block.error = read_pattern(parser);
   538	                                parser.allow_whitespace();
   539	                                parser.eat('}', true);
   540	                        }
   541	
   542	                        block.catch = create_fragment();
   543	                        parser.fragments.pop();
   544	                        parser.fragments.push(block.catch);
   545	
   546	                        return;
   547	                }
   548	
   549	                e.expected_token(start, '{:then ...} or {:catch ...}');
   550	        }
   551	
   552	        e.block_invalid_continuation_placement(start);
   553	}
   554	
   555	/** @param {Parser} parser */
   556	function close(parser) {
   557	        const start = parser.index - 1;
   558	
   559	        let block = parser.current();
   560	        /** Only relevant/reached for loose parsing mode */
   561	        let matched;
   562	
   563	        switch (block.type) {
   564	                case 'IfBlock':
   565	                        matched = parser.eat('if', true, false);
   566	
   567	                        if (!matched) {
   568	                                block.end = start - 1;
   569	                                parser.pop();
   570	                                close(parser);
   571	                                return;
   572	                        }
   573	
   574	                        parser.allow_whitespace();
   575	                        parser.eat('}', true);
   576	
   577	                        while (block.elseif) {
   578	                                block.end = parser.index;
   579	                                parser.stack.pop();
   580	                                block = /** @type {AST.IfBlock} */ (parser.current());
   581	                        }
   582	
   583	                        block.end = parser.index;
   584	                        parser.pop();
   585	                        return;
   586	
   587	                case 'EachBlock':
   588	                        matched = parser.eat('each', true, false);
   589	                        break;
   590	                case 'KeyBlock':
   591	                        matched = parser.eat('key', true, false);
   592	                        break;
   593	                case 'AwaitBlock':
   594	                        matched = parser.eat('await', true, false);
   595	                        break;
   596	                case 'SnippetBlock':
   597	                        matched = parser.eat('snippet', true, false);
   598	                        break;
   599	
   600	                case 'RegularElement':
   601	                        if (parser.loose) {
   602	                                matched = false;
   603	                        } else {
   604	                                // TODO handle implicitly closed elements
   605	                                e.block_unexpected_close(start);
   606	                        }
   607	                        break;
   608	
   609	                default:
   610	                        e.block_unexpected_close(start);
   611	        }
   612	
   613	        if (!matched) {
   614	                block.end = start - 1;
   615	                parser.pop();
   616	                close(parser);
   617	                return;
   618	        }
   619	
   620	        parser.allow_whitespace();
   621	        parser.eat('}', true);
   622	        block.end = parser.index;
   623	        parser.pop();
   624	}
   625

   230	        const parts = filename.split(/[/\\]/);
   231	        const basename = /** @type {string} */ (parts.pop());
   232	        const last_dir = /** @type {string} */ (parts.at(-1));
