    43	        'Math.tan': [NUMBER, Math.tan],
    44	        'Math.exp': [NUMBER, Math.exp],
    45	        'Math.log': [NUMBER, Math.log],
    46	        'Math.pow': [NUMBER, Math.pow],
    47	        'Math.sqrt': [NUMBER, Math.sqrt],
    48	        'Math.clz32': [NUMBER, Math.clz32],
    49	        'Math.imul': [NUMBER, Math.imul],
    50	        'Math.sign': [NUMBER, Math.sign],
    51	        'Math.log10': [NUMBER, Math.log10],
    52	        'Math.log2': [NUMBER, Math.log2],
    53	        'Math.log1p': [NUMBER, Math.log1p],
    54	        'Math.expm1': [NUMBER, Math.expm1],
    55	        'Math.cosh': [NUMBER, Math.cosh],
    56	        'Math.sinh': [NUMBER, Math.sinh],
    57	        'Math.tanh': [NUMBER, Math.tanh],
    58	        'Math.acosh': [NUMBER, Math.acosh],
    59	        'Math.asinh': [NUMBER, Math.asinh],
    60	        'Math.atanh': [NUMBER, Math.atanh],
    61	        'Math.trunc': [NUMBER, Math.trunc],
    62	        'Math.fround': [NUMBER, Math.fround],
    63	        'Math.cbrt': [NUMBER, Math.cbrt],
    64	        Number: [NUMBER, Number],
    65	        'Number.isInteger': [NUMBER, Number.isInteger],
    66	        'Number.isFinite': [NUMBER, Number.isFinite],
    67	        'Number.isNaN': [NUMBER, Number.isNaN],
    68	        'Number.isSafeInteger': [NUMBER, Number.isSafeInteger],
    69	        'Number.parseFloat': [NUMBER, Number.parseFloat],
    70	        'Number.parseInt': [NUMBER, Number.parseInt],
    71	        String: [STRING, String],
    72	        'String.fromCharCode': [STRING, String.fromCharCode],
    73	        'String.fromCodePoint': [STRING, String.fromCodePoint]
    74	};
    75	
    76	/** @type {Record<string, any>} */
    77	const global_constants = {
    78	        'Math.PI': Math.PI,
    79	        'Math.E': Math.E,
    80	        'Math.LN10': Math.LN10,
    81	        'Math.LN2': Math.LN2,
    82	        'Math.LOG10E': Math.LOG10E,
    83	        'Math.LOG2E': Math.LOG2E,
    84	        'Math.SQRT2': Math.SQRT2,
    85	        'Math.SQRT1_2': Math.SQRT1_2
    86	};
    87	
    88	export class Binding {
    89	        /** @type {Scope} */
    90	        scope;
    91	
    92	        /** @type {Identifier} */
    93	        node;
    94	
    95	        /** @type {BindingKind} */
    96	        kind;
    97	
    98	        /** @type {DeclarationKind} */
    99	        declaration_kind;
   100	
   101	        /**
   102	         * What the value was initialized with.
   103	         * For destructured props such as `let { foo = 'bar' } = $props()` this is `'bar'` and not `$props()`
   104	         * @type {null | Expression | FunctionDeclaration | ClassDeclaration | ImportDeclaration | AST.EachBlock | AST.SnippetBlock}
   105	         */
   106	        initial = null;
   107	
   108	        /** @type {Array<{ node: Identifier; path: AST.SvelteNode[] }>} */
   109	        references = [];
   110	
   111	        /**
   112	         * For `legacy_reactive`: its reactive dependencies
   113	         * @type {Binding[]}
   114	         */
   115	        legacy_dependencies = [];
   116	
   117	        /**
   118	         * Legacy props: the `class` in `{ export klass as class}`. $props(): The `class` in { class: klass } = $props()
   119	         * @type {string | null}
   120	         */
   121	        prop_alias = null;
   122	
   123	        /**
   124	         * Additional metadata, varies per binding type
   125	         * @type {null | { inside_rest?: boolean }}
   126	         */
   127	        metadata = null;
   128	
   129	        mutated = false;
   130	        reassigned = false;
   131	
   132	        /**
   133	         *
   134	         * @param {Scope} scope
   135	         * @param {Identifier} node
   136	         * @param {BindingKind} kind
   137	         * @param {DeclarationKind} declaration_kind
   138	         * @param {Binding['initial']} initial
   139	         */
   140	        constructor(scope, node, kind, declaration_kind, initial) {
   141	                this.scope = scope;
   142	                this.node = node;
   143	                this.initial = initial;
   144	                this.kind = kind;
   145	                this.declaration_kind = declaration_kind;
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        get updated() {
   149	                return this.mutated || this.reassigned;
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        /**
   153	         * @returns {this is Binding & { initial: ArrowFunctionExpression | FunctionDeclaration | FunctionExpression }}
   154	         */
   155	        is_function() {
   156	                if (this.updated) {
   157	                        // even if it's reassigned to another function,
   158	                        // we can't use it directly as e.g. an event handler
   159	                        return false;
   160	                }
   161	
   162	                const type = this.initial?.type;
   163	
   164	                return (
   165	                        type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' ||
   166	                        type === 'FunctionExpression' ||
   167	                        type === 'FunctionDeclaration'
   168	                );
   169	        }
   170	}
   171	
   172	class Evaluation {
   173	        /** @type {Set<any>} */
   174	        values;
   175	
   176	        /**
   177	         * True if there is exactly one possible value
   178	         * @readonly
   179	         * @type {boolean}
   180	         */
   181	        is_known = true;
   182	
   183	        /**
   184	         * True if the possible values contains `UNKNOWN`
   185	         * @readonly
   186	         * @type {boolean}
   187	         */
   188	        has_unknown = false;
   189	
   190	        /**
   191	         * True if the value is known to not be null/undefined
   192	         * @readonly
   193	         * @type {boolean}
   194	         */
   195	        is_defined = true;
   196	
   197	        /**
   198	         * True if the value is known to be a string
   199	         * @readonly
   200	         * @type {boolean}
   201	         */
   202	        is_string = true;
   203	
   204	        /**
   205	         * True if the value is known to be a number
   206	         * @readonly
   207	         * @type {boolean}
   208	         */
   209	        is_number = true;
   210	
   211	        /**
   212	         * True if the value is known to be a function
   213	         * @readonly
   214	         * @type {boolean}
   215	         */
   216	        is_function = true;
   217	
   218	        /**
   219	         * @readonly
   220	         * @type {any}
   221	         */
   222	        value = undefined;
   223	
   224	        /**
   225	         *
   226	         * @param {Scope} scope
   227	         * @param {Expression | FunctionDeclaration} expression
   228	         * @param {Set<any>} values
   229	         */
   230	        constructor(scope, expression, values) {
   231	                current_evaluations.set(expression, this);
   232	
   233	                this.values = values;
   234	
   235	                switch (expression.type) {
   236	                        case 'Literal': {
   237	                                this.values.add(expression.value);
   238	                                break;
   239	                        }
   240	
   241	                        case 'Identifier': {
   242	                                const binding = scope.get(expression.name);
   243	
   244	                                if (binding) {
   245	                                        if (
   246	                                                binding.initial?.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   247	                                                get_rune(binding.initial, scope) === '$props.id'
   248	                                        ) {
   249	                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   250	                                                break;
   251	                                        }
   252	
   253	                                        const is_prop =
   254	                                                binding.kind === 'prop' ||
   255	                                                binding.kind === 'rest_prop' ||
   256	                                                binding.kind === 'bindable_prop';
   257	
   258	                                        if (binding.initial?.type === 'EachBlock' && binding.initial.index === expression.name) {
   259	                                                this.values.add(NUMBER);
   260	                                                break;
   261	                                        }
   262	
   263	                                        if (!binding.updated && binding.initial !== null && !is_prop) {
   264	                                                binding.scope.evaluate(/** @type {Expression} */ (binding.initial), this.values);
   265	                                                break;
   266	                                        }
   267	                                } else if (expression.name === 'undefined') {
   268	                                        this.values.add(undefined);
   269	                                        break;
   270	                                }
   271	
   272	                                // TODO glean what we can from reassignments
   273	                                // TODO one day, expose props and imports somehow
   274	
   275	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   276	                                break;
   277	                        }
   278	
   279	                        case 'BinaryExpression': {
   280	                                const a = scope.evaluate(/** @type {Expression} */ (expression.left)); // `left` cannot be `PrivateIdentifier` unless operator is `in`
   281	                                const b = scope.evaluate(expression.right);
   282	
   283	                                if (a.is_known && b.is_known) {
   284	                                        this.values.add(binary[expression.operator](a.value, b.value));
   285	                                        break;
   286	                                }
   287	
   288	                                switch (expression.operator) {
   289	                                        case '!=':
   290	                                        case '!==':
   291	                                        case '<':
   292	                                        case '<=':
   293	                                        case '>':
   294	                                        case '>=':
   295	                                        case '==':
   296	                                        case '===':
   297	                                        case 'in':
   298	                                        case 'instanceof':
   299	                                                this.values.add(true);
   300	                                                this.values.add(false);
   301	                                                break;
   302	
   303	                                        case '%':
   304	                                        case '&':
   305	                                        case '*':
   306	                                        case '**':
   307	                                        case '-':
   308	                                        case '/':
   309	                                        case '<<':
   310	                                        case '>>':
   311	                                        case '>>>':
   312	                                        case '^':
   313	                                        case '|':
   314	                                                this.values.add(NUMBER);
   315	                                                break;
   316	
   317	                                        case '+':
   318	                                                if (a.is_string || b.is_string) {
   319	                                                        this.values.add(STRING);
   320	                                                } else if (a.is_number && b.is_number) {
   321	                                                        this.values.add(NUMBER);
   322	                                                } else {
   323	                                                        this.values.add(STRING);
   324	                                                        this.values.add(NUMBER);
   325	                                                }
   326	                                                break;
   327	
   328	                                        default:
   329	                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   330	                                }
   331	                                break;
   332	                        }
   333	
   334	                        case 'ConditionalExpression': {
   335	                                const test = scope.evaluate(expression.test);
   336	                                const consequent = scope.evaluate(expression.consequent);
   337	                                const alternate = scope.evaluate(expression.alternate);
   338	
   339	                                if (test.is_known) {
   340	                                        for (const value of (test.value ? consequent : alternate).values) {
   341	                                                this.values.add(value);
   342	                                        }
   343	                                } else {
   344	                                        for (const value of consequent.values) {
   345	                                                this.values.add(value);
   346	                                        }
   347	
   348	                                        for (const value of alternate.values) {
   349	                                                this.values.add(value);
   350	                                        }
   351	                                }
   352	                                break;
   353	                        }
   354	
   355	                        case 'LogicalExpression': {
   356	                                const a = scope.evaluate(expression.left);
   357	                                const b = scope.evaluate(expression.right);
   358	
   359	                                if (a.is_known) {
   360	                                        if (b.is_known) {
   361	                                                this.values.add(logical[expression.operator](a.value, b.value));
   362	                                                break;
   363	                                        }
   364	
   365	                                        if (
   366	                                                (expression.operator === '&&' && !a.value) ||
   367	                                                (expression.operator === '||' && a.value) ||
   368	                                                (expression.operator === '??' && a.value != null)
   369	                                        ) {
   370	                                                this.values.add(a.value);
   371	                                        } else {
   372	                                                for (const value of b.values) {
   373	                                                        this.values.add(value);
   374	                                                }
   375	                                        }
   376	
   377	                                        break;
   378	                                }
   379	
   380	                                for (const value of a.values) {
   381	                                        this.values.add(value);
   382	                                }
   383	
   384	                                for (const value of b.values) {
   385	                                        this.values.add(value);
   386	                                }
   387	                                break;
   388	                        }
   389	
   390	                        case 'UnaryExpression': {
   391	                                const argument = scope.evaluate(expression.argument);
   392	
   393	                                if (argument.is_known) {
   394	                                        this.values.add(unary[expression.operator](argument.value));
   395	                                        break;
   396	                                }
   397	
   398	                                switch (expression.operator) {
   399	                                        case '!':
   400	                                        case 'delete':
   401	                                                this.values.add(false);
   402	                                                this.values.add(true);
   403	                                                break;
   404	
   405	                                        case '+':
   406	                                        case '-':
   407	                                        case '~':
   408	                                                this.values.add(NUMBER);
   409	                                                break;
   410	
   411	                                        case 'typeof':
   412	                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   413	                                                break;
   414	
   415	                                        case 'void':
   416	                                                this.values.add(undefined);
   417	                                                break;
   418	
   419	                                        default:
   420	                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   421	                                }
   422	                                break;
   423	                        }
   424	
   425	                        case 'CallExpression': {
   426	                                const keypath = get_global_keypath(expression.callee, scope);
   427	
   428	                                if (keypath) {
   429	                                        if (is_rune(keypath)) {
   430	                                                const arg = /** @type {Expression | undefined} */ (expression.arguments[0]);
   431	
   432	                                                switch (keypath) {
   433	                                                        case '$state':
   434	                                                        case '$state.raw':
   435	                                                        case '$derived':
   436	                                                                if (arg) {
   437	                                                                        scope.evaluate(arg, this.values);
   438	                                                                } else {
   439	                                                                        this.values.add(undefined);
   440	                                                                }
   441	                                                                break;
   442	
   443	                                                        case '$props.id':
   444	                                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   445	                                                                break;
   446	
   447	                                                        case '$effect.tracking':
   448	                                                                this.values.add(false);
   449	                                                                this.values.add(true);
   450	                                                                break;
   451	
   452	                                                        case '$derived.by':
   453	                                                                if (arg?.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' && arg.body.type !== 'BlockStatement') {
   454	                                                                        scope.evaluate(arg.body, this.values);
   455	                                                                        break;
   456	                                                                }
   457	
   458	                                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   459	                                                                break;
   460	
   461	                                                        default: {
   462	                                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   463	                                                        }
   464	                                                }
   465	
   466	                                                break;
   467	                                        }
   468	
   469	                                        if (
   470	                                                Object.hasOwn(globals, keypath) &&
   471	                                                expression.arguments.every((arg) => arg.type !== 'SpreadElement')
   472	                                        ) {
   473	                                                const [type, fn] = globals[keypath];
   474	                                                const values = expression.arguments.map((arg) => scope.evaluate(arg));
   475	
   476	                                                if (fn && values.every((e) => e.is_known)) {
   477	                                                        this.values.add(fn(...values.map((e) => e.value)));
   478	                                                } else {
   479	                                                        this.values.add(type);
   480	                                                }
   481	
   482	                                                break;
   483	                                        }
   484	                                }
   485	
   486	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   487	                                break;
   488	                        }
   489	
   490	                        case 'TemplateLiteral': {
   491	                                let result = expression.quasis[0].value.cooked;
   492	
   493	                                for (let i = 0; i < expression.expressions.length; i += 1) {
   494	                                        const e = scope.evaluate(expression.expressions[i]);
   495	
   496	                                        if (e.is_known) {
   497	                                                result += e.value + expression.quasis[i + 1].value.cooked;
   498	                                        } else {
   499	                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   500	                                                break;
   501	                                        }
   502	                                }
   503	
   504	                                this.values.add(result);
   505	                                break;
   506	                        }
   507	
   508	                        case 'MemberExpression': {
   509	                                const keypath = get_global_keypath(expression, scope);
   510	
   511	                                if (keypath && Object.hasOwn(global_constants, keypath)) {
   512	                                        this.values.add(global_constants[keypath]);
   513	                                        break;
   514	                                }
   515	
   516	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   517	                                break;
   518	                        }
   519	
   520	                        case 'ArrowFunctionExpression':
   521	                        case 'FunctionExpression':
   522	                        case 'FunctionDeclaration': {
   523	                                this.values.add(FUNCTION);
   524	                                break;
   525	                        }
   526	
   527	                        default: {
   528	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   529	                        }
   530	                }
   531	
   532	                for (const value of this.values) {
   533	                        this.value = value; // saves having special logic for `size === 1`
   534	
   535	                        if (value !== STRING && typeof value !== 'string') {
   536	                                this.is_string = false;
   537	                        }
   538	
   539	                        if (value !== NUMBER && typeof value !== 'number') {
   540	                                this.is_number = false;
   541	                        }
   542	
   543	                        if (value !== FUNCTION) {
   544	                                this.is_function = false;
   545	                        }
   546	
   547	                        if (value == null || value === UNKNOWN) {
   548	                                this.is_defined = false;
   549	                        }
   550	
   551	                        if (value === UNKNOWN) {
   552	                                this.has_unknown = true;
   553	                        }
   554	                }
   555	
   556	                if (this.values.size > 1 || typeof this.value === 'symbol') {
   557	                        this.is_known = false;
   558	                }
   559	
   560	                current_evaluations.delete(expression);
   561	        }
   562	}
   563	
   564	export class Scope {
   565	        /** @type {ScopeRoot} */
   566	        root;
   567	
   568	        /**
   569	         * The immediate parent scope
   570	         * @type {Scope | null}
   571	         */
   572	        parent;
   573	
   574	        /**
   575	         * Whether or not `var` declarations are contained by this scope
   576	         * @type {boolean}
   577	         */
   578	        #porous;
   579	
   580	        /**
   581	         * A map of every identifier declared by this scope, and all the
   582	         * identifiers that reference it
   583	         * @type {Map<string, Binding>}
   584	         */
   585	        declarations = new Map();
   586	
   587	        /**
   588	         * A map of declarators to the bindings they declare
   589	         * @type {Map<VariableDeclarator | AST.LetDirective, Binding[]>}
   590	         */
   591	        declarators = new Map();
   592	
   593	        /**
   594	         * A set of all the names referenced with this scope
   595	         * — useful for generating unique names
   596	         * @type {Map<string, { node: Identifier; path: AST.SvelteNode[] }[]>}
   597	         */
   598	        references = new Map();
   599	
   600	        /**
   601	         * The scope depth allows us to determine if a state variable is referenced in its own scope,
   602	         * which is usually an error. Block statements do not increase this value
   603	         */
   604	        function_depth = 0;
   605	
   606	        /**
   607	         * If tracing of reactive dependencies is enabled for this scope
   608	         * @type {null | Expression}
   609	         */
   610	        tracing = null;
   611	
   612	        /**
   613	         *
   614	         * @param {ScopeRoot} root
   615	         * @param {Scope | null} parent
   616	         * @param {boolean} porous
   617	         */
   618	        constructor(root, parent, porous) {
   619	                this.root = root;
   620	                this.parent = parent;
   621	                this.#porous = porous;
   622	                this.function_depth = parent ? parent.function_depth + (porous ? 0 : 1) : 0;
   623	        }
   624	
   625	        /**
   626	         * @param {Identifier} node
   627	         * @param {Binding['kind']} kind
   628	         * @param {DeclarationKind} declaration_kind
   629	         * @param {null | Expression | FunctionDeclaration | ClassDeclaration | ImportDeclaration | AST.EachBlock | AST.SnippetBlock} initial
   630	         * @returns {Binding}
   631	         */
   632	        declare(node, kind, declaration_kind, initial = null) {
   633	                if (this.parent) {
   634	                        if (declaration_kind === 'var' && this.#porous) {
   635	                                return this.parent.declare(node, kind, declaration_kind);
   636	                        }
   637	
   638	                        if (declaration_kind === 'import') {
   639	                                return this.parent.declare(node, kind, declaration_kind, initial);
   640	                        }
   641	                }
   642	
   643	                if (this.declarations.has(node.name)) {
   644	                        const binding = this.declarations.get(node.name);
   645	                        if (binding && binding.declaration_kind !== 'var' && declaration_kind !== 'var') {
   646	                                // This also errors on function types, but that's arguably a good thing
   647	                                // declaring function twice is also caught by acorn in the parse phase
   648	                                e.declaration_duplicate(node, node.name);
   649	                        }
   650	                }
   651	
   652	                const binding = new Binding(this, node, kind, declaration_kind, initial);
   653	
   654	                validate_identifier_name(binding, this.function_depth);
   655	
   656	                this.declarations.set(node.name, binding);
   657	                this.root.conflicts.add(node.name);
   658	                return binding;
   659	        }
   660	
   661	        child(porous = false) {
   662	                return new Scope(this.root, this, porous);
   663	        }
   664	
   665	        /**
   666	         *<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

   840

   844	         */

   846	        const scope = new Scope(root, parent, false);
   847	        scopes.set(ast, scope);
   848

   868	        function add_params(scope, params) {
   869	                for (const param of params) {
   870	                        for (const node of extract_identifiers(param)) {
   871	                                scope.declare(node, 'normal', param.type === 'RestElement' ? 'rest_param' : 'param');
   872	                        }
   873	                }
   874	        }
   875	
   876	        /**
   877	         * @type {Visitor<Node, State, AST.SvelteNode>}
   878	         */
   879	        const create_block_scope = (node, { state, next }) => {
   880	                const scope = state.scope.child(true);
   881	                scopes.set(node, scope);
   882	
   883	                next({ scope });
   884	        };

   889	        const SvelteFragment = (node, { state, next }) => {

   891	                scopes.set(node, scope);
   892	                next({ scope });

   905	                }
   906	
   907	                const default_state = determine_slot(node)
   908	                        ? context.state
   909	                        : { scope: node.metadata.scopes.default };
   910	
   911	                for (const attribute of node.attributes) {
   912	                        if (attribute.type === 'LetDirective') {
   913	                                context.visit(attribute, default_state);
   914	                        } else {
   915	                                context.visit(attribute);
   916	                        }
   917	                }
   918	
   919	                for (const child of node.fragment.nodes) {
   920	                        let state = default_state;
   921	
   922	                        const slot_name = determine_slot(child);
   923	
   924	                        if (slot_name !== null) {
   925	                                node.metadata.scopes[slot_name] = context.state.scope.child();
   926	
   927	                                state = {
   928	                                        scope: node.metadata.scopes[slot_name]
   929	                                };
   930	                        }
   931	
   932	                        context.visit(child, state);
   933	                }
   934	        };
   935

   941

   943	                        visit(node.expression);
   944	                }

     1	/** @import { AwaitExpression, Expression, Property, SpreadElement } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { Context } from '../types' */
     3	import { dev, is_ignored } from '../../../../state.js';
     4	import * as b from '../../../../utils/builders.js';
     5	
     6	/**
     7	 * @param {AwaitExpression} node
     8	 * @param {Context} context
     9	 */
    10	export function AwaitExpression(node, context) {
    11	        const argument = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(node.argument));
    12	
    13	        const tla = context.state.is_instance && context.state.scope.function_depth === 1;
    14	
    15	        // preserve context for
    16	        //   a) top-level await and
    17	        //   b) awaits that precede other expressions in template or `$derived(...)`
    18	        if (tla || (is_reactive_expression(context) && !is_last_evaluated_expression(context, node))) {
    19	                return b.call(b.await(b.call('$.save', argument)));
    20	        }
    21	
    22	        // in dev, note which values are read inside a reactive expression,
    23	        // but don't track them
    24	        else if (dev && !is_ignored(node, 'await_reactivity_loss')) {
    25	                return b.call(b.await(b.call('$.track_reactivity_loss', argument)));
    26	        }
    27	
    28	        return argument === node.argument ? node : { ...node, argument };
    29	}
    30	
    31	/**
    32	 * @param {Context} context
    33	 */
    34	function is_reactive_expression(context) {
    35	        if (context.state.in_derived) {
    36	                return true;
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        let i = context.path.length;
    40	
    41	        while (i--) {
    42	                const parent = context.path[i];
    43	
    44	                if (
    45	                        parent.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' ||
    46	                        parent.type === 'FunctionExpression' ||
    47	                        parent.type === 'FunctionDeclaration'
    48	                ) {
    49	                        return false;
    50	                }
    51	
    52	                // @ts-expect-error we could probably use a neater/more robust mechanism
    53	                if (parent.metadata) {
    54	                        return true;
    55	                }
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        return false;
    59	}
    60	
    61	/**
    62	 * @param {Context} context
    63	 * @param {Expression | SpreadElement | Property} node
    64	 */
    65	function is_last_evaluated_expression(context, node) {
    66	        let i = context.path.length;
    67	
    68	        while (i--) {
    69	                const parent = /** @type {Expression | Property | SpreadElement} */ (context.path[i]);
    70	
    71	                // @ts-expect-error we could probably use a neater/more robust mechanism
    72	                if (parent.metadata) {
    73	                        return true;
    74	                }
    75	
    76	                switch (parent.type) {
    77	                        case 'ArrayExpression':
    78	                                if (node !== parent.elements.at(-1)) return false;
    79	                                break;
    80	
    81	                        case 'AssignmentExpression':
    82	                        case 'BinaryExpression':
    83	                        case 'LogicalExpression':
    84	                                if (node === parent.left) return false;
    85	                                break;
    86	
    87	                        case 'CallExpression':
    88	                        case 'NewExpression':
    89	                                if (node !== parent.arguments.at(-1)) return false;
    90	                                break;
    91	
    92	                        case 'ConditionalExpression':
    93	                                if (node === parent.test) return false;
    94	                                break;
    95	
    96	                        case 'MemberExpression':
    97	                                if (parent.computed && node === parent.object) return false;
    98	                                break;
    99	
   100	                        case 'ObjectExpression':
   101	                                if (node !== parent.properties.at(-1)) return false;
   102	                                break;
   103	
   104	                        case 'Property':
   105	                                if (node === parent.key) return false;
   106	                                break;
   107	
   108	                        case 'SequenceExpression':
   109	                                if (node !== parent.expressions.at(-1)) return false;
   110	                                break;
   111	
   112	                        case 'TaggedTemplateExpression':
   113	                                if (node !== parent.quasi.expressions.at(-1)) return false;
   114	                                break;
   115	
   116	                        case 'TemplateLiteral':
   117	                                if (node !== parent.expressions.at(-1)) return false;
   118	                                break;
   119	
   120	                        default:
   121	                                return false;
   122	                }
   123	
   124	                node = parent;
   125	        }
   126	}
   127

    13	/**
    14	 * A utility for extracting complex expressions (such as call expressions)
    15	 * from templates and replacing them with `$0`, `$1` etc
    16	 */
    17	export class Memoizer {
    18	        /** @type {Array<{ id: Identifier, expression: Expression }>} */
    19	        #sync = [];
    20	
    21	        /** @type {Array<{ id: Identifier, expression: Expression }>} */
    22	        #async = [];
    23	
    24	        /**
    25	         * @param {Expression} expression
    26	         * @param {boolean} has_await
    27	         */
    28	        add(expression, has_await) {
    29	                const id = b.id('#'); // filled in later
    30	
    31	                (has_await ? this.#async : this.#sync).push({ id, expression });
    32	
    33	                return id;
    34	        }
    35	
    36	        apply() {
    37	                return [...this.#async, ...this.#sync].map((memo, i) => {
    38	                        memo.id.name = `$${i}`;
    39	                        return memo.id;
    40	                });
    41	        }
    42	
    43	        deriveds(runes = true) {
    44	                return this.#sync.map((memo) =>
    45	                        b.let(memo.id, b.call(runes ? '$.derived' : '$.derived_safe_equal', b.thunk(memo.expression)))
    46	                );
    47	        }
    48	
    49	        async_ids() {
    50	                return this.#async.map((memo) => memo.id);
    51	        }
    52	
    53	        async_values() {
    54	                if (this.#async.length === 0) return;
    55	                return b.array(this.#async.map((memo) => b.thunk(memo.expression, true)));
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        sync_values() {
    59	                if (this.#sync.length === 0) return;
    60	                return b.array(this.#sync.map((memo) => b.thunk(memo.expression)));
    61	        }
    62	}
    63	
    64	/**
    65	 * @param {Array<AST.Text | AST.ExpressionTag>} values
    66	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    67	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
    68	 * @param {(value: Expression, metadata: ExpressionMetadata) => Expression} memoize
    69	 * @returns {{ value: Expression, has_state: boolean }}
    70	 */
    71	export function build_template_chunk(
    72	        values,
    73	        context,
    74	        state = context.state,
    75	        memoize = (value, metadata) =>
    76	                metadata.has_call || metadata.has_await ? state.memoizer.add(value, metadata.has_await) : value
    77	) {
    78	        /** @type {Expression[]} */
    79	        const expressions = [];
    80	
    81	        let quasi = b.quasi('');
    82	        const quasis = [quasi];
    83	
    84	        let has_state = false;
    85	        let has_await = false;
    86	
    87	        for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    88	                const node = values[i];
    89	
    90	                if (node.type === 'Text') {
    91	                        quasi.value.cooked += node.data;
    92	                } else if (node.expression.type === 'Literal') {
    93	                        if (node.expression.value != null) {
    94	                                quasi.value.cooked += node.expression.value + '';
    95	                        }
    96	                } else if (
    97	                        node.expression.type !== 'Identifier' ||
    98	                        node.expression.name !== 'undefined' ||
    99	                        state.scope.get('undefined')
   100	                ) {
   101	                        let value = memoize(
   102	                                build_expression(context, node.expression, node.metadata.expression, state),
   103	                                node.metadata.expression
   104	                        );
   105	
   106	                        const evaluated = state.scope.evaluate(value);
   107	
   108	                        has_await ||= node.metadata.expression.has_await;
   109	                        has_state ||= has_await || (node.metadata.expression.has_state && !evaluated.is_known);
   110	
   111	                        if (values.length === 1) {
   112	                                // If we have a single expression, then pass that in directly to possibly avoid doing
   113	                                // extra work in the template_effect (instead we do the work in set_text).
   114	                                if (evaluated.is_known) {
   115	                                        value = b.literal((evaluated.value ?? '') + '');
   116	                                }
   117	
   118	                                return { value, has_state };
   119	                        }
   120	
   121	                        if (
   122	                                value.type === 'LogicalExpression' &&
   123	                                value.right.type === 'Literal' &&
   124	                                (value.operator === '??' || value.operator === '||')
   125	                        ) {
   126	                                // `foo ?? null` -=> `foo ?? ''`
   127	                                // otherwise leave the expression untouched
   128	                                if (value.right.value === null) {
   129	                                        value = { ...value, right: b.literal('') };
   130	                                }
   131	                        }
   132	
   133	                        if (evaluated.is_known) {
   134	                                quasi.value.cooked += (evaluated.value ?? '') + '';
   135	                        } else {
   136	                                if (!evaluated.is_defined) {
   137	                                        // add `?? ''` where necessary
   138	                                        value = b.logical('??', value, b.literal(''));
   139	                                }
   140	
   141	                                expressions.push(value);
   142	
   143	                                quasi = b.quasi('', i + 1 === values.length);
   144	                                quasis.push(quasi);
   145	                        }
   146	                }
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        for (const quasi of quasis) {
   150	                quasi.value.raw = sanitize_template_string(/** @type {string} */ (quasi.value.cooked));
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        const value =
   154	                expressions.length > 0
   155	                        ? b.template(quasis, expressions)
   156	                        : b.literal(/** @type {string} */ (quasi.value.cooked));
   157	
   158	        return { value, has_state };
   159	}

   161	/**
   162	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
   163	 */
   164	export function build_render_statement(state) {
   165	        const { memoizer } = state;
   166	
   167	        const ids = memoizer.apply();
   168	
   169	        return b.stmt(
   170	                b.call(
   171	                        '$.template_effect',
   172	                        b.arrow(
   173	                                ids,
   174	                                state.update.length === 1 && state.update[0].type === 'ExpressionStatement'
   175	                                        ? state.update[0].expression
   176	                                        : b.block(state.update)
   177	                        ),
   178	                        memoizer.sync_values(),
   179	                        memoizer.async_values()
   180	                )
   181	        );
   182	}

   184	/**
   185	 * For unfortunate legacy reasons, directive names can look like this `use:a.b-c`
   186	 * This turns that string into a member expression
   187	 * @param {string} name
   188	 */
   189	export function parse_directive_name(name) {
   190	        // this allow for accessing members of an object
   191	        const parts = name.split('.');
   192	        let part = /** @type {string} */ (parts.shift());
   193	
   194	        /** @type {Identifier | MemberExpression} */
   195	        let expression = b.id(part);
   196	
   197	        while ((part = /** @type {string} */ (parts.shift()))) {
   198	                const computed = !regex_is_valid_identifier.test(part);
   199	                expression = b.member(expression, computed ? b.literal(part) : b.id(part), computed);
   200	        }
   201	
   202	        return expression;
   203	}
   204	
   205	/**
   206	 * Serializes `bind:this` for components and elements.
   207	 * @param {Identifier | MemberExpression | SequenceExpression} expression
   208	 * @param {Expression} value
   209	 * @param {import('zimmerframe').Context<AST.SvelteNode, ComponentClientTransformState>} context
   210	 */
   211	export function build_bind_this(expression, value, { state, visit }) {
   212	        if (expression.type === 'SequenceExpression') {
   213	                const [get, set] = /** @type {SequenceExpression} */ (visit(expression)).expressions;
   214	                return b.call('$.bind_this', value, set, get);
   215	        }
   216	
   217	        /** @type {Identifier[]} */
   218	        const ids = [];
   219	
   220	        /** @type {Expression[]} */
   221	        const values = [];
   222	
   223	        /** @type {string[]} */
   224	        const seen = [];
   225	
   226	        const transform = { ...state.transform };
   227	
   228	        // Pass in each context variables to the get/set functions, so that we can null out old values on teardown.
   229	        // Note that we only do this for each context variables, the consequence is that the value might be stale in
   230	        // some scenarios where the value is a member expression with changing computed parts or using a combination of multiple
   231	        // variables, but that was the same case in Svelte 4, too. Once legacy mode is gone completely, we can revisit this.
   232	        walk(expression, null, {
   233	                Identifier(node, { path }) {
   234	                        if (seen.includes(node.name)) return;
   235	                        seen.push(node.name);
   236	
   237	                        const parent = /** @type {Expression} */ (path.at(-1));
   238	                        if (!is_reference(node, parent)) return;
   239	
   240	                        const binding = state.scope.get(node.name);
   241	                        if (!binding) return;
   242	
   243	                        for (const [owner, scope] of state.scopes) {
   244	                                if (owner.type === 'EachBlock' && scope === binding.scope) {
   245	                                        ids.push(node);
   246	                                        values.push(/** @type {Expression} */ (visit(node)));
   247	
   248	                                        if (transform[node.name]) {
   249	                                                transform[node.name] = {
   250	                                                        ...transform[node.name],
   251	                                                        read: (node) => node
   252	                                                };
   253	                                        }
   254	
   255	                                        break;
   256	                                }
   257	                        }
   258	                }
   259	        });
   260	
   261	        const child_state = { ...state, transform };
   262	
   263	        const get = /** @type {Expression} */ (visit(expression, child_state));
   264	        const set = /** @type {Expression} */ (
   265	                visit(b.assignment('=', expression, b.id('$$value')), child_state)
   266	        );
   267	
   268	        // If we're mutating a property, then it might already be non-existent.
   269	        // If we make all the object nodes optional, then it avoids any runtime exceptions.
   270	        /** @type {Expression | Super} */
   271	        let node = get;
   272	
   273	        while (node.type === 'MemberExpression') {
   274	                node.optional = true;
   275	                node = node.object;
   276	        }
   277	
   278	        return b.call(
   279	                '$.bind_this',
   280	                value,
   281	                b.arrow([b.id('$$value'), ...ids], set),
   282	                b.arrow([...ids], get),
   283	                values.length > 0 && b.thunk(b.array(values))
   284	        );
   285	}
   286	
   287	/**
   288	 * @param {ComponentClientTransformState} state
   289	 * @param {AST.BindDirective} binding
   290	 * @param {MemberExpression} expression
   291	 */
   292	export function validate_binding(state, binding, expression) {
   293	        if (binding.expression.type === 'SequenceExpression') {
   294	                return;
   295	        }
   296	        // If we are referencing a $store.foo then we don't need to add validation
   297	        const left = object(binding.expression);
   298	        const left_binding = left && state.scope.get(left.name);
   299	        if (left_binding?.kind === 'store_sub') return;
   300	
   301	        const loc = locator(binding.start);
   302	
   303	        const obj = /** @type {Expression} */ (expression.object);
   304	
   305	        state.init.push(
   306	                b.stmt(
   307	                        b.call(
   308	                                '$.validate_binding',
   309	                                b.literal(state.analysis.source.slice(binding.start, binding.end)),
   310	                                b.thunk(
   311	                                        state.store_to_invalidate ? b.sequence([b.call('$.mark_store_binding'), obj]) : obj
   312	                                ),
   313	                                b.thunk(
   314	                                        /** @type {Expression} */ (
   315	                                                expression.computed
   316	                                                        ? expression.property
   317	                                                        : b.literal(/** @type {Identifier} */ (expression.property).name)
   318	                                        )
   319	                                ),
   320	                                loc && b.literal(loc.line),
   321	                                loc && b.literal(loc.column)
   322	                        )
   323	                )
   324	        );
   325	}
   326	
   327	/**
   328	 * In dev mode validate mutations to props
   329	 * @param {AssignmentExpression | UpdateExpression} node
   330	 * @param {Context} context
   331	 * @param {Expression} expression
   332	 */
   333	export function validate_mutation(node, context, expression) {
   334	        let left = /** @type {Expression | Super} */ (
   335	                node.type === 'AssignmentExpression' ? node.left : node.argument
   336	        );
   337	
   338	        if (!dev || left.type !== 'MemberExpression' || is_ignored(node, 'ownership_invalid_mutation')) {
   339	                return expression;
   340	        }
   341	
   342	        const name = object(left);
   343	        if (!name) return expression;
   344	
   345	        const binding = context.state.scope.get(name.name);
   346	        if (binding?.kind !== 'prop' && binding?.kind !== 'bindable_prop') return expression;
   347	
   348	        const state = /** @type {ComponentClientTransformState} */ (context.state);
   349	        state.analysis.needs_mutation_validation = true;
   350	
   351	        /** @type {Array<Identifier | Literal | Expression>} */
   352	        const path = [];
   353	
   354	        while (left.type === 'MemberExpression') {
   355	                if (left.property.type === 'Literal') {
   356	                        path.unshift(left.property);
   357	                } else if (left.property.type === 'Identifier') {
   358	                        const transform = Object.hasOwn(context.state.transform, left.property.name)
   359	                                ? context.state.transform[left.property.name]
   360	                                : null;
   361	                        if (left.computed) {
   362	                                path.unshift(transform?.read ? transform.read(left.property) : left.property);
   363	                        } else {
   364	                                path.unshift(b.literal(left.property.name));
   365	                        }
   366	                } else {
   367	                        return expression;
   368	                }
   369	
   370	                left = left.object;
   371	        }
   372	
   373	        path.unshift(b.literal(name.name));
   374	
   375	        const loc = locator(/** @type {number} */ (left.start));
   376	
   377	        return b.call(
   378	                '$$ownership_validator.mutation',
   379	                b.literal(binding.prop_alias),
   380	                b.array(path),
   381	                expression,
   382	                loc && b.literal(loc.line),
   383	                loc && b.literal(loc.column)
   384	        );
   385	}
   386	
   387	/**
   388	 *
   389	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   390	 * @param {Expression} expression
   391	 * @param {ExpressionMetadata} metadata
   392	 */
   393	export function build_expression(context, expression, metadata, state = context.state) {
   394	        const value = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(expression, state));
   395	
   396	        // Components not explicitly in legacy mode might be expected to be in runes mode (especially since we didn't
   397	        // adjust this behavior until recently, which broke people's existing components), so we also bail in this case.
   398	        // Kind of an in-between-mode.
   399	        if (context.state.analysis.runes || context.state.analysis.maybe_runes) {
   400	                return value;
   401	        }
   402	
   403	        if (!metadata.has_call && !metadata.has_member_expression && !metadata.has_assignment) {
   404	                return value;
   405	        }
   406	
   407	        // Legacy reactivity is coarse-grained, looking at the statically visible dependencies. Replicate that here
   408	        const sequence = b.sequence([]);
   409	
   410	        for (const binding of metadata.references) {
   411	                if (binding.kind === 'normal' && binding.declaration_kind !== 'import') {
   412	                        continue;
   413	                }
   414	
   415	                var getter = build_getter({ ...binding.node }, state);
   416	
   417	                if (
   418	                        binding.kind === 'bindable_prop' ||
   419	                        binding.kind === 'template' ||
   420	                        binding.declaration_kind === 'import' ||
   421	                        binding.node.name === '$$props' ||
   422	                        binding.node.name === '$$restProps'
   423	                ) {
   424	                        getter = b.call('$.deep_read_state', getter);
   425	                }
   426	
   427	                sequence.expressions.push(getter);
   428	        }
   429	
   430	        sequence.expressions.push(b.call('$.untrack', b.thunk(value)));
   431	
   432	        return sequence;
   433	}
   434	
   435	/**
   436	 * Wraps a statement/expression with dev stack tracking in dev mode
   437	 * @param {Expression} expression - The function call to wrap (e.g., $.if, $.each, etc.)
   438	 * @param {{ start?: number }} node - AST node for location info
   439	 * @param {'component' | 'if' | 'each' | 'await' | 'key' | 'render'} type - Type of block/component
   440	 * @param {Record<string, number | string>} [additional] - Any additional properties to add to the dev stack entry
   441	 * @returns {ExpressionStatement} - Statement with or without dev stack wrapping
   442	 */
   443	export function add_svelte_meta(expression, node, type, additional) {
   444	        if (!dev) {
   445	                return b.stmt(expression);
   446	        }
   447	
   448	        const location = node.start !== undefined && locator(node.start);
   449	        if (!location) {
   450	                return b.stmt(expression);
   451	        }
   452	
   453	        return b.stmt(
   454	                b.call(
   455	                        '$.add_svelte_meta',
   456	                        b.arrow([], expression),
   457	                        b.literal(type),
   458	                        b.id(component_name),
   459	                        b.literal(location.line),
   460	                        b.literal(location.column),
   461	                        additional && b.object(Object.entries(additional).map(([k, v]) => b.init(k, b.literal(v))))
   462	                )
   463	        );
   464	}

     1	/** @import { ArrowFunctionExpression, FunctionExpression, Node } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../../types' */
     3	import { build_hoisted_params } from '../../utils.js';
     4	
     5	/**
     6	 * @param {ArrowFunctionExpression | FunctionExpression} node
     7	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
     8	 */
     9	export const visit_function = (node, context) => {
    10	        const metadata = node.metadata;
    11	
    12	        let state = { ...context.state, in_constructor: false, in_derived: false };
    13	
    14	        if (node.type === 'FunctionExpression') {
    15	                const parent = /** @type {Node} */ (context.path.at(-1));
    16	                state.in_constructor = parent.type === 'MethodDefinition' && parent.kind === 'constructor';
    17	        }
    18	
    19	        if (metadata?.hoisted === true) {
    20	                const params = build_hoisted_params(node, context);
    21	
    22	                return /** @type {FunctionExpression} */ ({
    23	                        ...node,
    24	                        params,
    25	                        body: context.visit(node.body, state)
    26	                });
    27	        }
    28	
    29	        context.next(state);
    30	};

     1	/** @import { Node } from 'esrap/languages/ts' */
     2	/** @import { ValidatedCompileOptions, CompileResult, ValidatedModuleCompileOptions } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ComponentAnalysis, Analysis } from '../types' */
     4	import { print } from 'esrap';
     5	import ts from 'esrap/languages/ts';
     6	import { VERSION } from '../../../version.js';
     7	import { server_component, server_module } from './server/transform-server.js';
     8	import { client_component, client_module } from './client/transform-client.js';
     9	import { render_stylesheet } from './css/index.js';
    10	import { merge_with_preprocessor_map, get_source_name } from '../../utils/mapped_code.js';
    11	import * as state from '../../state.js';
    12	
    13	/**
    14	 * @param {ComponentAnalysis} analysis
    15	 * @param {string} source
    16	 * @param {ValidatedCompileOptions} options
    17	 * @returns {CompileResult}
    18	 */
    19	export function transform_component(analysis, source, options) {
    20	        if (options.generate === false) {
    21	                return {
    22	                        js: /** @type {any} */ (null),
    23	                        css: null,
    24	                        warnings: state.warnings, // set afterwards
    25	                        metadata: {
    26	                                runes: analysis.runes
    27	                        },
    28	                        ast: /** @type {any} */ (null) // set afterwards
    29	                };
    30	        }
    31	
    32	        const program =
    33	                options.generate === 'server'
    34	                        ? server_component(analysis, options)
    35	                        : client_component(analysis, options);
    36	
    37	        const js_source_name = get_source_name(options.filename, options.outputFilename, 'input.svelte');
    38	
    39	        const js = print(/** @type {Node} */ (program), ts({ comments: analysis.comments }), {
    40	                // include source content; makes it easier/more robust looking up the source map code
    41	                // (else esrap does return null for source and sourceMapContent which may trip up tooling)
    42	                sourceMapContent: source,
    43	                sourceMapSource: js_source_name
    44	        });
    45	
    46	        merge_with_preprocessor_map(js, options, js_source_name);
    47	
    48	        const css =
    49	                analysis.css.ast && !analysis.inject_styles
    50	                        ? render_stylesheet(source, analysis, options)
    51	                        : null;
    52	
    53	        return {
    54	                js,
    55	                css,
    56	                warnings: state.warnings, // set afterwards. TODO apply preprocessor sourcemap
    57	                metadata: {
    58	                        runes: analysis.runes
    59	                },
    60	                ast: /** @type {any} */ (null) // set afterwards
    61	        };
    62	}
    63	
    64	/**
    65	 * @param {Analysis} analysis
    66	 * @param {string} source
    67	 * @param {ValidatedModuleCompileOptions} options
    68	 * @returns {CompileResult}
    69	 */
    70	export function transform_module(analysis, source, options) {
    71	        if (options.generate === false) {
    72	                return {
    73	                        js: /** @type {any} */ (null),
    74	                        css: null,
    75	                        warnings: state.warnings, // set afterwards
    76	                        metadata: {
    77	                                runes: true
    78	                        },
    79	                        ast: /** @type {any} */ (null) // set afterwards
    80	                };
    81	        }
    82	
    83	        const program =
    84	                options.generate === 'server'
    85	                        ? server_module(analysis, options)
    86	                        : client_module(analysis, options);
    87	
    88	        const basename = options.filename.split(/[/\\]/).at(-1);
    89	        if (program.body.length > 0) {
    90	                program.body[0].leadingComments = [
    91	                        {
    92	                                type: 'Block',
    93	                                value: ` ${basename} generated by Svelte v${VERSION} `
    94	                        }
    95	                ];
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        const js = print(/** @type {Node} */ (program), ts({ comments: analysis.comments }), {
    99	                // include source content; makes it easier/more robust looking up the source map code
   100	                // (else esrap does return null for source and sourceMapContent which may trip up tooling)
   101	                sourceMapContent: source,
   102	                sourceMapSource: get_source_name(options.filename, undefined, 'input.svelte.js')
   103	        });
   104	
   105	        // prepend comment
   106	        js.code = `/* ${basename} generated by Svelte v${VERSION} */\n${js.code}`;
   107	        js.map.mappings = ';' + js.map.mappings;
   108	
   109	        return {
   110	                js,
   111	                css: null,
   112	                metadata: {
   113	                        runes: true
   114	                },
   115	                warnings: state.warnings, // set afterwards
   116	                ast: /** @type {any} */ (null) // set afterwards
   117	        };
   118	}
   119

    64	/** @type {Visitors} */

    66	        _: function set_scope(node, { next, state }) {
    67	                const scope = state.scopes.get(node);
    68	
    69	                if (scope && scope !== state.scope) {
    70	                        const transform = { ...state.transform };
    71	
    72	                        for (const [name, binding] of scope.declarations) {
    73	                                if (
    74	                                        binding.kind === 'normal' ||
    75	                                        // Reads of `$state(...)` declarations are not
    76	                                        // transformed if they are never reassigned
    77	                                        (binding.kind === 'state' && !is_state_source(binding, state.analysis))
    78	                                ) {
    79	                                        delete transform[name];
    80	                                }
    81	                        }
    82	
    83	                        next({ ...state, transform, scope });
    84	                } else {
    85	                        next();
    86	                }

   142	
   143	/**
   144	 * @param {ComponentAnalysis} analysis
   145	 * @param {ValidatedCompileOptions} options
   146	 * @returns {ESTree.Program}
   147	 */
   148	export function client_component(analysis, options) {
   149	        /** @type {ComponentClientTransformState} */
   150	        const state = {
   151	                analysis,
   152	                options,
   153	                scope: analysis.module.scope,
   154	                scopes: analysis.module.scopes,
   155	                is_instance: false,
   156	                hoisted: [b.import_all('$', 'svelte/internal/client')],
   157	                node: /** @type {any} */ (null), // populated by the root node
   158	                legacy_reactive_imports: [],
   159	                legacy_reactive_statements: new Map(),
   160	                metadata: {
   161	                        namespace: options.namespace,
   162	                        bound_contenteditable: false
   163	                },
   164	                events: new Set(),
   165	                preserve_whitespace: options.preserveWhitespace,
   166	                state_fields: new Map(),
   167	                transform: {},
   168	                in_constructor: false,
   169	                in_derived: false,
   170	                instance_level_snippets: [],
   171	                module_level_snippets: [],
   172	
   173	                // these are set inside the `Fragment` visitor, and cannot be used until then
   174	                init: /** @type {any} */ (null),
   175	                update: /** @type {any} */ (null),
   176	                after_update: /** @type {any} */ (null),

   182	                walk(/** @type {AST.SvelteNode} */ (analysis.module.ast), state, visitors)
   183	        );

   186	                ...state,
   187	                transform: { ...state.transform },
   188	                scope: analysis.instance.scope,
   189	                scopes: analysis.instance.scopes,
   190	                is_instance: true

   194	                walk(/** @type {AST.SvelteNode} */ (analysis.instance.ast), instance_state, visitors)
   195	        );
   196	
   197	        const template = /** @type {ESTree.Program} */ (
   198	                walk(
   199	                        /** @type {AST.SvelteNode} */ (analysis.template.ast),
   200	                        {
   201	                                ...state,

   216	        /** @type {ESTree.VariableDeclaration[]} */
   217	        const legacy_reactive_declarations = [];

   219	        let needs_store_cleanup = false;
   220	
   221	        for (const [name, binding] of analysis.instance.scope.declarations) {
   222	                if (binding.kind === 'legacy_reactive') {

   231	                        if (store_setup.length === 0) {

    13	export function CallExpression(node, context) {
    14	        const rune = get_rune(node, context.state.scope);
    15	
    16	        switch (rune) {
    17	                case '$host':
    18	                        return b.id('$$props.$$host');
    19	
    20	                case '$effect.tracking':
    21	                        return b.call('$.effect_tracking');
    22	
    23	                // transform state field assignments in constructors
    24	                case '$state':
    25	                case '$state.raw': {
    26	                        let arg = node.arguments[0];
    27	
    28	                        /** @type {Expression | undefined} */
    29	                        let value = undefined;
    30	
    31	                        if (arg) {
    32	                                value = /** @type {Expression} */ (context.visit(node.arguments[0]));
    33	
    34	                                if (
    35	                                        rune === '$state' &&
    36	                                        should_proxy(/** @type {Expression} */ (arg), context.state.scope)
    37	                                ) {

    39	                                }
    40	                        }
    41	
    42	                        return b.call('$.state', value);
    43	                }
    44	
    45	                case '$derived':
    46	                case '$derived.by': {
    47	                        let fn = /** @type {Expression} */ (

    49	                        );
    50

     1	/** @import { Pattern } from 'estree' */
     2	/** @import { AST } from '#compiler' */
     3	/** @import { ComponentContext } from '../types' */
     4	import { dev } from '../../../../state.js';
     5	import { extract_identifiers } from '../../../../utils/ast.js';
     6	import * as b from '#compiler/builders';
     7	import { create_derived } from '../utils.js';
     8	import { get_value } from './shared/declarations.js';
     9	import { build_expression } from './shared/utils.js';
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * @param {AST.ConstTag} node
    13	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
    14	 */
    15	export function ConstTag(node, context) {
    16	        const declaration = node.declaration.declarations[0];
    17	        // TODO we can almost certainly share some code with $derived(...)
    18	        if (declaration.id.type === 'Identifier') {
    19	                const init = build_expression(context, declaration.init, node.metadata.expression, {
    20	                        ...context.state,
    21	                        in_derived: true
    22	                });
    23	                let expression = create_derived(context.state, b.thunk(init));
    24	
    25	                if (dev) {
    26	                        expression = b.call('$.tag', expression, b.literal(declaration.id.name));
    27	                }
    28	
    29	                context.state.init.push(b.const(declaration.id, expression));
    30	
    31	                context.state.transform[declaration.id.name] = { read: get_value };
    32	
    33	                // we need to eagerly evaluate the expression in order to hit any
    34	                // 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
    35	                if (dev) {
    36	                        context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.get', declaration.id)));
    37	                }
    38	        } else {
    39	                const identifiers = extract_identifiers(declaration.id);
    40	                const tmp = b.id(context.state.scope.generate('computed_const'));
    41	
    42	                const transform = { ...context.state.transform };
    43	
    44	                // Make all identifiers that are declared within the following computed regular
    45	                // variables, as they are not signals in that context yet
    46	                for (const node of identifiers) {
    47	                        delete transform[node.name];
    48	                }
    49	
    50	                const child_state = { ...context.state, transform };
    51	
    52	                // TODO optimise the simple `{ x } = y` case — we can just return `y`
    53	                // instead of destructuring it only to return a new object
    54	                const init = build_expression(
    55	                        { ...context, state: child_state },
    56	                        declaration.init,
    57	                        node.metadata.expression,
    58	                        { ...child_state, in_derived: true }
    59	                );
    60	                const fn = b.arrow(
    61	                        [],
    62	                        b.block([
    63	                                b.const(/** @type {Pattern} */ (context.visit(declaration.id, child_state)), init),
    64	                                b.return(b.object(identifiers.map((node) => b.prop('init', node, node))))
    65	                        ])
    66	                );
    67	
    68	                let expression = create_derived(context.state, fn);
    69	
    70	                if (dev) {
    71	                        expression = b.call('$.tag', expression, b.literal('[@const]'));
    72	                }
    73	
    74	                context.state.init.push(b.const(tmp, expression));
    75	
    76	                // we need to eagerly evaluate the expression in order to hit any
    77	                // 'Cannot access x before initialization' errors
    78	                if (dev) {
    79	                        context.state.init.push(b.stmt(b.call('$.get', tmp)));
    80	                }
    81	
    82	                for (const node of identifiers) {
    83	                        context.state.transform[node.name] = {
    84	                                read: (node) => b.member(b.call('$.get', tmp), node)
    85	                        };
    86	                }
    87	        }
    88	}
